1448 "gentians, as fresh and shining as if they were growing on the"
1448 "spot. She clasped her hands, enraptured with their beauty."
1448 ""
1448 "\"How exquisite! what a lovely sight!\" she exclaimed. \"Heidi,"
1448 "dearest child, come here! Is it you who have prepared this"
1448 "pleasure for me? It is perfectly wonderful!\""
1448 ""
1448 "The children ran up."
1448 ""
1448 "\"No, no, I did not put them there,\" said Heidi, \"but I know who"
1448 "did.\""
1448 ""
1448 "\"They grow just like that on the mountain, grandmamma, only if"
1448 "anything they look more beautiful still,\" Clara put in; \"but"
1448 "guess who brought those down to-day,\" and as she spoke she gave"
1448 "such a pleased smile that the grandmother thought for a moment"
1448 "the child herself must have gathered them. But that was hardly"
1448 "possible."
1448 ""
1448 "At this moment a slight rustling was heard behind the fir trees."
1448 "It was Peter, who had just arrived. He had made a long round,"
1448 "having seen from the distance who it was standing beside Uncle"
1448 "in front of the hut, and he was trying to slip by unobserved. But"
1448 "grandmamma had seen and recognized him, and suddenly the thought"
1448 "struck her that it might be Peter who had brought the flowers"
1448 "and that he was now trying to get away unseen, feeling shy about"
1448 "it; but she could not let him go off like that, he must have some"
1448 "little reward."
1448 ""
1448 "\"Come along, boy; come here, do not be afraid,\" she called to"
1448 "him."
1448 ""
1448 "Peter stood still, petrified with fear. After all he had gone"
1448 "through that day he felt he had no longer any power of"
1448 "resistance left. All he could think was, \"It's all up with me"
1448 "now.\" Every hair of his head stood on end, and he stepped forth"
1448 "from behind the fir trees, his face pale and distorted with"
1448 "terror."
1448 ""
1448 "\"Courage, boy,\" said grandmamma in her effort to dispel his"
1448 "shyness, \"tell me now straight out without hesitation, was it"
1448 "you who did it?\""
1448 ""
1448 "Peter did not lift his eyes and therefore did not see at what"
1448 "grandmamma was pointing. But he knew that Uncle was standing at"
1448 "the corner of the hut, fixing him with his grey eyes, while"
1448 "beside him stood the most terrible person that Peter could"
1448 "conceive--the police-constable from Frankfurt. Quaking in every"
1448 "limb, and with trembling lips he muttered a low, \"Yes.\""
1448 ""
1448 "\"Well, and what is there dreadful about that?\" said grandmamma."
1448 ""
1448 "\"Because--because--it is all broken to pieces and no one can put"
1448 "it together again.\" Peter brought out his words with difficulty,"
1448 "and his knees knocked together so that he could hardly stand."
1448 ""
1448 "Grandmamma went up to Uncle. \"Is that poor boy a little out of"
1448 "his mind?\" she asked sympathisingly."
1448 ""
1448 "\"Not in the least,\" Uncle assured her, \"it is only that he was"
1448 "the wind that sent the chair rolling down the slope, and he is"
1448 "expecting his well-deserved punishment.\""
1448 ""
1448 "Grandmamma found this hard to believe, for in her opinion Peter"
1448 "did not look an entirely bad boy, nor could he have any reason"
1448 "for destroying such a necessary thing as the chair. But Uncle"
1448 "had only given expression to the suspicion that he had from the"
1448 "moment the accident happened. The angry looks which Peter had"
1448 "from the beginning cast at Clara, and the other signs of his"
1448 "dislike to what had been taking place on the mountain, had not"
1448 "escaped Uncle's eye. Putting two and two together he had come to"
1448 "the right conclusion as to the cause of the disaster, and he"
1448 "therefore spoke without hesitation when he accused Peter. The"
1448 "lady broke into lively expostulations on hearing this."
1448 ""
1448 "\"No, no, dear Uncle, we will not punish the poor boy any"

1448 "possession, and a possession well worth having too, and he is"

1448 "And saying this she went back to Peter, who still stood"
1448 "frightened and trembling. She sat down on the seat under the fir"
1448 "trees and called him to her kindly,--"
1448 ""
1448 "\"Come here, boy, and stand in front of me, for I have something"
1448 "to say to you. Leave off shaking and trembling, for I want you"
1448 "to listen to me. You sent the chair rolling down the mountain so"
1448 "that it was broken to pieces. That was a very wrong thing to do,"
1448 "as you yourself knew very well at the time, and you also knew"
1448 "that you deserved to be punished for it, and in order to escape"
1448 "this you have been doing all you can to hide the truth from"
1448 "everybody. But be sure of this, Peter: that those who do wrong"
1448 "make a mistake when they think no one knows anything about it."
1448 "For God sees and hears everything, and when the wicked doer"
1448 "tries to hide what he has done, then God wakes up a little"
1448 "watchman that He places inside us all when we are born and who"
1448 "sleeps on quietly till we do something wrong. And the little"
1448 "watchman has a small goad in his hand, And when he wakes up he"
1448 "keeps on pricking us with it, so that we have not a moment's"
1448 "peace. And the watchman torments us still further, for he keeps"
1448 "on calling out, 'Now you will be found out! Now they will drag"
1448 "you off to punishment!' And so we pass our life in fear and"
1448 "trouble, and never know a moment's happiness or peace. Have you"
1448 "not felt something like that lately, Peter?\""
1448 ""
1448 "Peter gave a contrite nod of the head, as one who knew all about"
1448 "it, for grandmamma had described his own feelings exactly."
1448 ""

1448 "to go in and yet wanted so much to see the flowers, she made the"

1448 "good out of evil for those whom you meant to injure, and you who"

1448 "goad and his disagreeable voice. Will you remember all this?\""
1448 ""

1448 "constable was still standing with the Uncle."
1448 ""
1448 "\"That's right, and now the thing is over and done for,\" said"

1448 ""
1448 "Peter lifted his head at this, and stared open-eyed at"

1448 ""

1448 ""

1448 ""

1448 ""

1448 ""

1448 ""

1448 ""

1448 ""

1448 ""

1448 ""

1448 ""

1448 "There is a great deal of building going on at Dorfli. The doctor"
